# Events for the Three Kingdoms

# Centralized monarchy of Goguryeo
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_SAMGUK.1
	title = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.1.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.1.d"
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
        tag = GOG
        is_year = 60
		NOT = { is_year = 70 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
    }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 700
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.1.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		GOG = {
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = autocracy_reform
			set_government_rank = 2
			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = 10
			grant_independence = yes
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Buyeo"
				change_adm = 3
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 3
				age = 25
				claim = 95
				regency = yes
			}
			define_heir = {
				name = "Gung"
				dynasty = "Go"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 5
				age = 7
				claim = 95
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = OKJ
			}
		}
		GAY = {
			clr_country_flag = eh_override_name
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = tribal_kingdom
			set_government_rank = 2
			add_prestige = 10
			restore_country_name = yes
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Suro"
				dynasty = "Kim"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 3
				claim = 95
				age = 20
			}
			define_heir = {
				dynasty = "Kim"
			}
		}
	}
}

# Three clans
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_SAMGUK.3
	title = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.3.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.3.d"
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		SLL = { was_player = yes }
        is_year = 280
		NOT = { is_year = 290 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
    }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 700
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.3.a" # Park
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SLL = {
			add_legitimacy = 10
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = "Park"
			}
			define_heir = {
				dynasty = "Park"
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.3.b" # Seok
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		SLL = {
			add_prestige = 10
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = "Seok"
			}
			define_heir = {
				dynasty = "Seok"
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.3.c" # Kim
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		SLL = {
			add_stability = 1
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = "Kim"
			}
			define_heir = {
				dynasty = "Kim"
			}
		}
	}
}

# Setting on the Three Kingdoms
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_SAMGUK.4
	title = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.4.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.4.d"
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		ROOT = { culture_group = korean_g }
        is_year = 2
		NOT = { is_year = 40 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
    }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			south_korea_area = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { province_id = 2741 }
				}
				change_culture = jinhan
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = writing
					value = 100
				}
			}
			eastern_korea_area = {
				change_culture = jinhan
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = writing
					value = 100
				}
			}
			western_korea_area = {
				change_culture = buyeo
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = writing
					value = 100
				}
			}
			hamgyeong_area = { change_culture = buyeo }
			pyongan_area = {
				change_culture = buyeo
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = writing
					value = 100
				}
			}
			jilin_area = {
				change_culture = buyeo
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = writing
					value = 100
				}
			}
			liaoning_area = { change_culture = chihan }
			733 = { rename_capital = "Zhenfan" }
			1845 = { rename_capital = "Chaoxian" }
			2744 = { rename_capital = "Anping" }
			4231 = { rename_capital = "Daifang" }
			2111 = { rename_capital = "Jolbon" }
			4201 = { rename_capital = "Gungnae" }
			1850 = {
				rename_capital = "Yeongju"
				change_culture = manchu
			}
			4564 = { rename_capital = "Gaseopwon" }
			732 = { rename_capital = "Biyeol" }
			734 = { rename_capital = "Bugwon" }
			736 = { rename_capital = "Dalgubeol" }
			737 = { rename_capital = "Geumma" }
			2694 = { rename_capital = "Haseula" }
			4227 = { rename_capital = "Geumgwan" }
			4228 = { rename_capital = "Bala" }
			4229 = { rename_capital = "Sabeol" }
			4230 = { rename_capital = "Namhansan" }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.4.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SLL = { 
			set_country_flag = eh_override_name
			override_country_name = "Gyerim" 
		}
		GAY = {
			set_country_flag = gaya_event_fired
			set_country_flag = eh_override_name
			override_country_name = "Byeonhan"
		}
	}
}

# Three Kingdoms
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_SAMGUK.5
	title = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.5.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.5.d"
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = BUY
			tag = DBY
			tag = DON
			tag = MHN
			tag = GAY
			tag = TAM
		}
        is_year = 390
		NOT = { is_year = 400 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
    }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 700
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.5.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				BUY = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = GOG
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				DBY = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = GOG
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				DON = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = GOG
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MHN = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = GOG
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GAY = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = GOG
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TAM = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = GOG
		}
	}
	
	option = {

			}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TAM = { was_player = yes }

	option = {

		}

			limit = {
				MHN = { was_player = yes }

# Aftermath of the Goguryeo-Wei War
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_SAMGUK.6
	title = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.6.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.6.d"
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.6.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		WEI = {
			clr_country_flag = sanguo_china
			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = 10
			add_mandate = 10
			add_manpower = 10
			add_war_exhaustion = -1
			white_peace = GOG
			white_peace = DON
			white_peace = MHN
			country_event = { id = eh_asia_CHN.9 days = 1 }
		}
		GOG = {
			clr_country_flag = sanguo_china
			add_stability = -1
			add_prestige = -10
			add_manpower = -10
			add_war_exhaustion = 1
			inherit = OKJ
			manchuria_region = {
				limit = { owned_by = GOG }
				add_devastation = 30
			}
		}
		DON = {
			clr_country_flag = sanguo_china
			add_stability = -1
			add_prestige = -10
			add_manpower = -10
			add_war_exhaustion = 1
		}
		MHN = {
			clr_country_flag = sanguo_china
			add_stability = -1
			add_prestige = -10
			add_manpower = -10
			add_war_exhaustion = 1
		}
		BKJ = {
			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = 10
			add_manpower = 10
			grant_independence = yes
		}
		SLL = { inherit = JHN }
	}
}

# Conquering Chinese Commanderies
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_SAMGUK.7
	title = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.7.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.7.d"
	picture = CONQUEST_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GOG = {
				pyongan_area = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = GOG }
					}
					cede_province = GOG
					add_core = GOG
					remove_core = A12
				}
				western_korea_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = GOG }
							NOT = { province_id = 735 }
							NOT = { province_id = 4230 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = GOG
					add_core = GOG
					remove_core = A12
				}
				730 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = GOG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = GOG
					add_core = GOG
					remove_core = BUY
				}
				2112 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = GOG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = GOG
					add_core = GOG
					remove_core = A12
				}
				4661 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = GOG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = GOG
					add_core = GOG
					remove_core = BUY
				}
			}
			BKJ = {
				grant_independence = yes
				1013 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = BKJ }
						}
					}
					cede_province = BKJ
					add_core = BKJ
					remove_core = MHN
				}
				4229 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = BKJ }
						}
					}
					cede_province = BKJ
					add_core = BKJ
					remove_core = MHN
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.7.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		GOG = {
			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = 10
			grant_independence = yes
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Eulbul"
				dynasty = "Go"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 5
				claim = 95
				age = 15
			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 3	shock = 3	manuever = 0	siege = 2	}
			define_consort = {
				dynasty = "Ju"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			remove_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
			733 = { rename_capital = "Jaeryong" }
			1845 = { rename_capital = "Pyongyang" }
			2744 = { rename_capital = "Anpyeong" }
			4231 = { rename_capital = "Songak" }
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = DON
			}
		}
	}
}

# Geunchogo of Baekje
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_SAMGUK.8
	title = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.8.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.8.d"
	picture = COURT_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
        tag = BKJ
        is_year = 345
		NOT = { is_year = 355 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
    }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 700
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			BKJ = {
				737 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = BKJ }
						}
					}
					cede_province = BKJ
					add_core = BKJ
					remove_core = MHN
				}
				4231 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = BKJ }
						}
					}
					cede_province = BKJ
					add_core = BKJ
				}
				735 = {
					add_institution_embracement = {
						which = caste_system
						value = 100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.8.a" 
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		BKJ = {
			add_adm_power = 100
			add_dip_power = 100
			add_mil_power = 100
			add_stability = 1

			add_sailors = 1000
			add_prestige = 30
			add_years_of_income = 3
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			create_alliance = KYU
			create_alliance = YAM

				who = KYU
				value = 25
				mutual = yes
			}

				who = YAM
				value = 25

			}

				name = "Gu"

			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 3	shock = 3	manuever = 1	siege = 0	}
			define_consort = {
				dynasty = "Jin"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			define_heir = {
				name = "Su"
				dynasty = "Buyeo"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 4
				claim = 95
				age = 1
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = MHN
			}
		}
		SLL = {
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = autocracy_reform
			set_government_rank = 2
			define_heir = {
				name = "Naemul"
				dynasty = "Kim"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 1
				claim = 95
			}
			define_consort = {
				name = "Boban"
				dynasty = "Kim"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			2745 = {
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = caste_system
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
		GOG = {
			pyongan_area = {
				limit = { owned_by = GOG }

			}

# Gwanggaeto the Great
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_SAMGUK.9
	title = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.9.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.9.d"
	picture = COURT_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
        tag = GOG
        is_year = 391
		NOT = { is_year = 395 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
    }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GOG = {
				liaoning_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = GOG }
					}
					add_core = GOG
				}
				jilin_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = GOG }
					}
					cede_province = GOG
					add_core = GOG
					remove_core = BUY
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_SAMGUK.9.a"  
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		GOG = {
			set_country_flag = samguk_korea
			add_adm_power = 100
			add_dip_power = 100
			add_mil_power = 100
			add_stability = 1
			add_manpower = 30
			add_sailors = 1000
			add_prestige = 30
			add_years_of_income = 3
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			create_guarantee = SLL
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Damdeok"
				dynasty = "Go"
				change_adm = 5
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 6
				age = 18
				claim = 95
			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 4	shock = 4	manuever = 2	siege = 1	}
			define_heir = {
				name = "Georyeon"
				dynasty = "Go"
				change_adm = 5
				change_dip = 5
				change_mil = 5
				age = 1
				claim = 95
			}
			726 = {
				han_banner = GOG
				han_banner = GOG
				han_banner = GOG
				han_banner = GOG
				manchu_banner = GOG
				manchu_banner = GOG
				manchu_banner = GOG
				manchu_banner = GOG
			}
			country_event = { id = eh_korea_SAMGUK.10 days = 700 }
		}
		YAN = {
			set_country_flag = samguk_korea
			add_stability = -1
			add_prestige = -10
			add_manpower = -10
			add_army_tradition = -10
			add_army_professionalism = -0.1
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = GOG
				casus_belli = cb_annex
			}
		}
		BKJ = {
			set_country_flag = samguk_korea
			add_stability = -1

# Silla-Tang War
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.1
	title = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.1.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.1.d"
	picture = BATTLE_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = SLL
		is_year = 673
		NOT = { is_year = 676 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			SLL = {
				south_korea_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = SLL }
							NOT = { province_id = 2741 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = SLL
					add_core = SLL
					remove_core = TNG
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {

		}
		TNG = {

# Rise of the Balhae
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.3
	title = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.3.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.3.d"
	picture = COURT_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SLL
		is_year = 698
		NOT = { is_year = 700 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			SMM = {
				change_tag = BLH
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = autocracy_reform
				set_government_rank = 2
				set_capital = 2108
				swap_free_idea_group = yes
				change_primary_culture = buyeo
				add_accepted_culture = manchu
				add_adm_power = 100
				add_dip_power = 100
				add_mil_power = 100
				add_stability = 1
				add_manpower = 30
				add_sailors = 1000
				add_prestige = 30
				add_years_of_income = 3
				change_religion = mahayana
				change_technology_group = early_chinese
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Jo-yeong"
					dynasty = "Dae"
					change_adm = 4
					change_dip = 4
					change_mil = 5	
					claim = 95
					age = 49
				}
				define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 3	shock = 3	manuever = 1	siege = 0	}
				define_heir = {
					dynasty = "Dae"
				}
				jilin_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = BLH }
					}
					cede_province = BLH
					add_core = BLH
					remove_core = TNG
				}
				furdan_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = BLH }
					}
					cede_province = BLH
					add_core = BLH
					remove_core = SMM
				}
				ningguta_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = BLH }
							NOT = { province_id = 731 }
							NOT = { province_id = 4663 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = BLH
					add_core = BLH
					remove_core = SMM
				}
				hamgyeong_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = BLH }

						}
					}
					cede_province = BLH
					add_core = BLH
					remove_core = SMM

					}

					add_core = BLH

				}
				2111 = { rename_capital = "Seogyeong" }
			}
			SLL = {
				add_liberty_desire = -100
				add_trust = {
					who = TNG
					value = 25
					mutual = yes
				}
			}
			TNG = {
				create_subject = {
					subject_type = tributary_state
					subject = SLL
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.3.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {

		}
	}

	}

# Jang Bogo
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.6
	title = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.6.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.6.d"
	picture = SHIP_SAILING_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
        tag = SLL
        is_year = 820
		NOT = { is_year = 830 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
    }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 700
	}
	
	option = { # Have him lead our navy!
		name = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.6.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
		SLL = {
			add_sailors = 1000
			add_navy_tradition = 10
			define_admiral = {
				name = "Jang Bogo"
				shock = 3
				fire = 3
				manuever = 4
				siege = 0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Hire him as an advisor!
		name = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.6.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		SLL = {
			add_sailors = 1000
			add_navy_tradition = 10
			define_advisor = {
				type = statesman
				name = "Jang Bogo"
				culture = korean
				skill = 3
				discount = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Don't intervene in the trial
		name = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.6.c"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		SLL = { add_stability_or_adm_power = yes }
	}
}

# Decline of the Silla
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.7
	title = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.7.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.7.d"
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
        tag = SLL
        is_year = 880
		NOT = { is_year = 890 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
    }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 700
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.7.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SLL = {
			set_country_flag = uprising_eh
			add_adm_power = -100
			add_dip_power = -100
			add_mil_power = -100
			add_stability = -1
			add_corruption = 10
			add_inflation = 1
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Man"
				dynasty = "Kim"
				change_adm = 0
				change_dip = 0
				change_mil = 0
				female = yes
				claim = 95
				age = 25
			}
			define_consort = {
				name = "Wihong"
				dynasty = "Kim"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = no
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				add_unrest = 0.1
				add_devastation = 10
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = anti_tax_rebels
					size = 1
				}
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = anti_tax_rebels
					size = 1
				}
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = anti_tax_rebels
					size = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Rise of the Later Baekje
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.8
	title = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.8.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.8.d"
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
        tag = SLL
		is_year = 890
		NOT = { is_year = 895 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
    }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			SLL = {
				add_stability = -1
				add_corruption = 10
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = warlordism
					duration = 2000
				}
				every_owned_province = { add_unrest = -0.9 }
				country_event = { id = eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.9 days = 100 }
			}
			BKJ = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = warlord_state
				set_government_rank = 1
				set_capital = 737
				change_primary_culture = korean
				south_korea_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = {	owned_by = BKJ }
							NOT = { province_id = 1013 }
							NOT = { province_id = 2741 }
							NOT = { province_id = 4229 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = BKJ
					add_core = BKJ
					remove_core = SLL
				}
			}
			SMJ = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = warlord_state
				set_government_rank = 1
				2694 = {
					if = {
						limit = { owned_by = SLL }
					}
					cede_province = SMJ
					add_core = SMJ
					remove_core = SLL
				}
			}
			SSA = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = warlord_state
				set_government_rank = 1
				set_capital = 734
				734 = {
					if = {
						limit = { owned_by = SLL }
					}
					cede_province = SSA
					add_core = SSA
					remove_core = SLL
				}
				735 = {
					if = {
						limit = { owned_by = SLL }
					}
					cede_province = SSA
					add_core = SSA
					remove_core = SLL
				}
			}
			SSB = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = warlord_state
				set_government_rank = 1
				4229 = {
					if = {
						limit = { owned_by = SLL }
					}
					cede_province = SSB
					add_core = SSB
					remove_core = SLL
				}
			}
			SPS = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = warlord_state
				set_government_rank = 1
				change_primary_culture = korean
				set_capital = 4231
				733 = {
					if = {
						limit = { owned_by = SLL }
					}
					change_culture = korean
					cede_province = SPS
					add_core = SPS
					remove_core = SLL
				}
				4231 = {
					if = {
						limit = { owned_by = SLL }
					}
					change_culture = korean
					cede_province = SPS
					add_core = SPS
					remove_core = SLL
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.8.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SLL = { 
			clr_country_flag = uprising_eh
			add_treasury = -10000
		}
		BKJ = {
			change_primary_culture = korean
			add_treasury = 10000
			add_years_of_income = 1
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Hwon"
				dynasty = "Gyeon"
				change_adm = 0
				change_dip = 1
				change_mil = 6	
				claim = 95
				age = 23
			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 3	shock = 3	manuever = 1	siege = 0	}
		}
		SMJ = {
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Sun-sik"
				dynasty = "Kim"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 3	
				claim = 95
			}
		}
		SSA = {
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Gil"
				dynasty = "Yang"
				change_adm = 0
				change_dip = 1
				change_mil = 4	
				claim = 95
			}
		}
		SSB = {
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Ajagae"
				dynasty = "Yi"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 3	
				claim = 95
			}
		}
		SPS = {
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Ryung"
				dynasty = "Wang"
				change_adm = 3
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 3	
				claim = 95
			}
			define_consort = {
				name = "Wisuk"
				dynasty = "Han"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Strange prince
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.9
	title = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.9.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.9.d"
	picture = NEW_HEIR_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.9.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SLL = {
			add_stability = -1
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		GOG = {
			set_country_flag = eh_override_name
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = chinese_warlord
			set_government_rank = 1
			set_capital = 4231
			change_primary_culture = korean
			override_country_name = "Goryeo"
			add_adm_tech = 7
			add_dip_tech = 7
			add_mil_tech = 7
			inherit = SMJ
			732 = {
				if = {
					limit = { owned_by = SLL }
				}
				cede_province = GOG
				add_core = GOG
				remove_core = SLL
			}
			2694 = {
				if = {
					limit = { owned_by = SMJ }
				}
				cede_province = GOG
				add_core = GOG
				remove_core = SMJ
			}
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Gung-ye"
				dynasty = "Kim"
				change_adm = 1
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 4	
				claim = 95
				age = 21
			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 3	shock = 2	manuever = 0	siege = 1	}
			define_consort = {
				dynasty = "Gang"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.9.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		SLL = {
			add_stability = -2
			add_corruption = 20
			add_treasury = -10000
			define_heir = {
				name = "Gung-ye"
				dynasty = "Kim"
				change_adm = 1
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 4	
				claim = 10
				age = 21
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = pretender_rebels
					size = 1
				}
			}
		}
		GOG = {
			add_treasury = 10000
			add_years_of_income = 1
		}
	}
}

# Notable dynasty - House of Kim
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.10
	title = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.10.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.10.d"
	picture = COURT_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		tag = SLL
		government = monarchy
		has_regency = no
		is_year = 360
		NOT = { is_year = 935 }
		NOT = { dynasty = "Kim" }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_NAMBUKGUK.10.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		ROOT = {
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = "Kim"
				male = yes
			}
			define_heir = {
				dynasty = "Kim"
				male = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Later Three Kingdoms
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.1
	title = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.1.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.1.d"
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			tag = SLL
			exists = BKJ
			exists = GOG
		}
        is_year = 900
		NOT = { is_year = 905 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
    }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			SLL = { remove_country_modifier = warlordism }
			GOG = {
				set_country_flag = eh_override_name
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = autocracy_reform
				set_government_rank = 2
				set_capital = 2694
				add_adm_power = 100
				add_dip_power = 100
				add_mil_power = 100
				add_stability = 1
				add_manpower = 30
				add_sailors = 1000
				add_prestige = 30
				add_treasury = 10000
				add_years_of_income = 3
				add_army_tradition = 10
				add_army_professionalism = 0.1
				grant_independence = yes
				inherit = SPS
				inherit = SSA
				every_owned_province = { add_unrest = -0.9 }
				override_country_name = "Taebong"
				western_korea_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = GOG }
					}
					cede_province = GOG
					add_core = GOG
					remove_core = SPS
				}
				eastern_korea_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = GOG }
							NOT = { province_id = 2745 }
							NOT = { province_id = 4227 }
							NOT = { province_id = 736 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = GOG
					add_core = GOG
					remove_core = SSB
				}
				732 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = GOG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = GOG
					add_core = GOG
					remove_core = SSB
				}
				1845 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = GOG }
						}
					}
					cede_province = GOG
					add_core = GOG
					remove_core = BLH
				}
			}
			BKJ = {
				change_government = monarchy
				add_government_reform = autocracy_reform
				set_government_rank = 2
				add_adm_power = 100
				add_dip_power = 100
				add_mil_power = 100
				add_stability = 1
				add_manpower = 30
				add_sailors = 1000
				add_prestige = 30
				add_treasury = 10000
				add_years_of_income = 3
				add_army_tradition = 10
				add_army_professionalism = 0.1
				grant_independence = yes
				create_subject = {
					subject_type = tributary_state
					subject = SSA
				}
				south_korea_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = {	owned_by = BKJ }
							NOT = { province_id = 2741 }
							NOT = { province_id = 4229 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = BKJ
					add_core = BKJ
					remove_core = SLL
				}
				create_subject = {
					subject_type = tributary_state
					subject = SSA
				}
				create_subject = {
					subject_type = tributary_state
					subject = TAM
				}
			}
			BLH = {
				add_adm_power = -100
				add_dip_power = -100
				add_mil_power = -100
				add_stability = -1
				add_manpower = -10
				add_inflation = 1
			}
			KHT = {
				inherit = KMX
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Abaoji"
					dynasty = "Yelu"
					change_adm = 4
					change_dip = 4
					change_mil = 5
					claim = 95
					age = 35
				}
				define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 4	shock = 4	manuever = 2	siege = 2 }
				define_consort = {
					name = "Ping"
					dynasty = "Shulu"
					change_adm = 4
					change_dip = 4
					change_mil = 4
					female = yes
				}
				define_heir = {
					name = "Deguang"
					dynasty = "Yelu"
					change_adm = 3
					change_dip = 3
					change_mil = 5
					claim = 95
				}
				chahar_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = KHT }
					}
					cede_province = KHT
					add_core = KHT
					remove_core = KMX
				}
				703 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = KHT }
						}
					}
					cede_province = KHT
					add_core = KHT
					remove_core = KMX
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_subject_of = BKJ }
				add_liberty_desire = -100
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.1.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				SLL = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = GOG
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.1.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				SLL = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = BKJ
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.1.c"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

# Rise of the Goryeo
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.2
	title = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.2.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.2.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GOG = {
				every_owned_province = {
					add_core = GOR
					remove_core = GOG
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.2.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		GOR = {
			add_adm_power = 100
			add_dip_power = 100
			add_mil_power = 100
			add_stability = 1
			add_manpower = 30
			add_sailors = 1000
			add_meritocracy_effect = yes
			add_prestige = 30
			add_treasury = 30000
			add_years_of_income = 3
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			set_capital = 4231
			create_guarantee = SLL
			swap_free_idea_group = yes
			inherit = GOG
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Geon"
				dynasty = "Wang"
				change_adm = 5
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 6	
				claim = 95
				age = 40
			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {	fire = 4	shock = 4	manuever = 1	siege = 1	}
			define_consort = {
				name = "Janghwa"
				dynasty = "Oh"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			define_heir = {
				dynasty = "Wang"
				male = yes
			}
			add_trust = {
				who = SLL
				value = 25
				mutual = yes
			}
			add_trust = {
				who = BLH
				value = 25
				mutual = yes
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = SLL
				modifier = sided_with_us
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = BLH
				modifier = sided_with_us
			}
		}
		BKJ = {
			inherit = SSA
			4229 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = BKJ }
					}
				}
				cede_province = BKJ
				add_core = BKJ
				remove_core = SSA
			}
		}

# Fall of the Balhae
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.3
	title = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.3.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.3.d"
	picture = MONGOL_BANNERS_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			BLH = {
				change_tag = DND
				change_primary_culture = khitan
				add_accepted_culture = buyeo
				define_ruler = {
					dynasty = "Yelu"
				}
				2107 = { rename_capital = "Dongjingcheng" }
				1850 = { rename_capital = "Furdan" }
				4564 = { rename_capital = "Fu'erhe" }
			}
			BKJ = {
				4227 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = BKJ }
						}
					}
					cede_province = BKJ
					add_core = BKJ
					remove_core = SLL
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.3.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		LIO = {
			clr_country_flag = balhae_conquest
			add_prestige = 10
			add_stability = 1
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			add_years_of_income = 2
			white_peace = DND
			2744 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = LIO }
					}
				}
				cede_province = LIO
				add_core = LIO
				remove_core = DND
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = client_kingdom
				subject = DND
			}
		}
		DND = {
			clr_country_flag = balhae_conquest
			add_liberty_desire = -100
		}
		JEO = {
			2111 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = JEO }
					}
				}
				cede_province = JEO
				add_core = JEO
				remove_core = DND
			}
			4201 = {

					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = JEO }
					}
				}
				cede_province = JEO
				add_core = JEO
				remove_core = DND
			}
			4232 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = JEO }
					}
				}
				cede_province = JEO
				add_core = JEO
				remove_core = DND
			}
			define_ruler = {
				dynasty = "Dae"
			}
			define_heir = {
				dynasty = "Yeol"
			}
		}
	}
}

# Fall of the millennium kingdom
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.4
	title = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.4.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.4.d"
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GOR
		is_year = 935
		NOT = { is_year = 937 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GOR = {
				set_country_flag = goryeo_unification
				inherit = SLL
				eastern_korea_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = GOR }
							NOT = { province_id = 4227 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = GOR
					add_core = GOR
					remove_core = SLL
				}
				create_subject = {
					subject_type = tributary_state
					subject = TAM
				}
				country_event = { id = eh_korea_GOR.1 days = 300 }
			}
			BKJ = {
				set_country_flag = goryeo_unification
				add_stability = -1
				add_corruption = 10
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Singeom"
					dynasty = "Gyeon"
					change_adm = 0
					change_dip = 0
					change_mil = 1	
					claim = 95
					age = 40
				}
				remove_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
				declare_war_with_cb = {
					who = GOR
					casus_belli = cb_annex
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.4.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				BKJ = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = GOR
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.4.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

					limit = {

							NOT = { owned_by = GOR }

						}
					}
					cede_province = GOR
					add_core = GOR
					remove_core = BKJ
				}
				732 = { rename_capital = "Hamju" }
				733 = { rename_capital = "Hwangju" }
				734 = { rename_capital = "Wonju" }
				735 = { rename_capital = "Yangju" }
				736 = { rename_capital = "Daegu" }
				737 = { rename_capital = "Jeonju" }
				1013 = { rename_capital = "Gongju" }
				1845 = { rename_capital = "Seogyeong" }
				2694 = { rename_capital = "Gangneung" }
				2744 = { rename_capital = "Guju" }
				2745 = { rename_capital = "Donggyeong" }
				4227 = { rename_capital = "Jinju" }
				4228 = { rename_capital = "Naju" }
				4229 = { rename_capital = "Chungju" }
				4230 = { rename_capital = "Suju" }
				4231 = { rename_capital = "Gaegyeong" }
			}
		}
	}

# Jurchen expedition
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_GOR.9
	title = "eh_korea_GOR.9.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_GOR.9.d"
	picture = COLONIZATION_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GOR
		is_year = 1115
		NOT = { is_year = 1120 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HSM = {
				add_stability = 1
				add_prestige = 10
				add_army_tradition = 10
				add_army_professionalism = 0.1
				add_treasury = 5000
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Wuyashu"
					dynasty = "Wanggiya"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 4
					change_mil = 6
					age = 45
					claim = 95
				}
				define_consort = {
					name = "Jingxi"
					dynasty = "Tangkuo"
					change_adm = 2
					change_dip = 2
					change_mil = 2
					female = yes
				}
				define_heir = {
					name = "Aguda"
					dynasty = "Wanggiya"
					change_adm = 3
					change_dip = 4
					change_mil = 6
					age = 33
					claim = 95
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_GOR.9.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		GOR = {
			add_treasury = -5000
			add_prestige = -10
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_GOR.9.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		GOR = {
			set_country_flag = jurchen_expedition_korea
			add_treasury = -5000
			2743 = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { owned_by = GOR }
					}
				}
				cede_province = GOR
				add_core = GOR
			}
		}
		HSM = {
			set_country_flag = jurchen_expedition_korea
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = GOR
				casus_belli = cb_conquest
				war_goal_province = 2743
			}
		}
	}
}

# Mongol invasions of Korea (1)
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_GOR.13
	title = "eh_korea_GOR.13.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_GOR.13.d"
	picture = MONGOL_BANNERS_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			MGE = {
				inherit = XIE
				manchuria_region = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = MGE }
							NOT = { area = east_heilongjiang_area }
							NOT = { area = central_ilin_hala_area }
							NOT = { area = ilan_hala_area }
						}
					}
					cede_province = MGE
					add_core = MGE
					remove_core = XIE
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_GOR.13.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		GOR = {
			set_country_flag = mongol_invasion_korea
			add_stability = -1
			add_corruption = 10
			add_army_tradition = -10
			add_army_professionalism = -0.1
			define_general = {
				name = "Park Seo"
				shock = 3
				fire = 3
				manuever = 1
				siege = 3
			}
			country_event = { id = eh_korea_GOR.14 days = 100 }
		}
		MGE = {
			set_country_flag = mongol_invasion_korea
			define_general = {
				name = "Saritai"
				shock = 3
				fire = 3
				manuever = 3
				siege = 0
			}
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = GOR
				casus_belli = cb_force_tributary
			}
			country_event = { id = eh_asia_MON.54 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_GOR.13.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		GOR = {
			add_stability = -1
			add_corruption = 10
			add_prestige = -10
			add_army_tradition = -10
			add_army_professionalism = -0.1
		}
		MGE = {
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = tributary_state
				subject = GOR
			}
		}
	}
}

# Last reform
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_GOR.21
	title = "eh_korea_GOR.21.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_GOR.21.d"
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GOR
		is_year = 1355
		NOT = { is_year = 1360 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GOR = {
				732 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = GOR }
						}
					}
					change_culture = korean
					cede_province = GOR
					add_core = GOR
					remove_core = YUA
				}
				2743 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = GOR }
						}
					}
					change_culture = korean
					cede_province = GOR
					add_core = GOR
					remove_core = YUA
				}
				735 = { rename_capital = "Hanyang" }
				1845 = { rename_capital = "Pyongyang" }
				2744 = { rename_capital = "Uiju" }
				2745 = { rename_capital = "Gyeongju" }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_GOR.21.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		GOR = {
			add_adm_power = 100
			add_dip_power = 100
			add_mil_power = 100
			add_stability = 1
			add_manpower = 30
			add_prestige = 30
			add_liberty_desire = 50
			add_years_of_income = 3
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			grant_independence = yes
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Jeon"
				dynasty = "Wang"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 3
				change_mil = 5
				claim = 95
				age = 21
			}
			define_consort = {
				name = "Budashiri"
				dynasty = "Borjigin"
				culture = mongol
				change_adm = 3
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 4
				female = yes
				age = 20
			}
			remove_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
			define_general = {
				name = "Choe Yeong"
				shock = 3
				fire = 4
				manuever = 2
				siege = 0
			}
		}
		YUA = {
			add_mandate = -10
			add_prestige = -10
			break_marriage = GOR
		}

# Rise of the Joseon dynasty
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_JOS.1
	title = "eh_korea_JOS.1.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_JOS.1.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GOR = {
				every_owned_province = {
					add_core = KOR
					remove_core = GOR
				}
				732 = { rename_capital = "Hamheung" }
				735 = { rename_capital = "Hanseong" }
				4230 = { rename_capital = "Suwon" }
				4231 = { rename_capital = "Kaesong" }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_JOS.1.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		KOR = {
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = korean_monarchy
			set_government_rank = 2
			add_adm_power = 100
			add_dip_power = 100
			add_mil_power = 100
			add_stability = 3
			add_manpower = 30
			add_meritocracy_effect = yes
			add_prestige = 30
			add_treasury = 50000
			add_years_of_income = 3
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			add_inflation = -3
			change_religion = confucianism
			add_harmonized_religion = mahayana
			set_capital = 735
			swap_free_idea_group = yes
			inherit = GOR
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Seong-gye"
				dynasty = "Yi"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 4
				change_mil = 6	
				claim = 95
				age = 57
			}
			define_consort = {
				name = "Sindeok"
				dynasty = "Gang"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			define_advisor = {
				type = statesman
				name = "Jeong Do-jeon"
				culture = korean
				skill = 3
				discount = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = "eh_korea_JOS.19.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_JOS.19.d"
	picture = BATTLE_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_JOS.19.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		KOR = {
			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = 10
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			add_war_exhaustion = 2
			set_capital = 735
			define_general = {
				name = "Gwon Yul"
				shock = 3
				fire = 3
				manuever = 1
				siege = 1
				trait = master_of_arms_personality
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { province_id = 2745 }
						NOT = { province_id = 4227 }
						NOT = { province_id = 736 }
					}
				}
				change_controller = KOR
			}
			2744 = { remove_building = fort_17th }
		}
		TYT = {
			add_prestige = -10
			add_war_exhaustion = 1
		}
		MNG = {
			add_manpower = -50
			add_army_tradition = -10
			add_army_professionalism = -0.1

	title = "eh_korea_JOS.33.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_JOS.33.d"
	picture = CORRUPTION_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
		
	trigger = {
		tag = KOR
		is_year = 1800
		NOT = { is_year = 1810 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 700
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_JOS.33.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		KOR = {
			add_prestige = -20
			add_stability = -1
			add_corruption = 20
			add_inflation = 2
			add_adm_power = -50
			add_dip_power = -50
			add_mil_power = -50
			remove_faction = dongin_korea
			remove_faction = seoin_korea
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Gong"
				dynasty = "Yi"
				change_adm = 1
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				age = 10
				claim = 95
			}
			define_consort = {
				name = "Sunwon"
				dynasty = "Kim"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			remove_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
		}
	}
}

# Hong Gyeong-nae Rebellion
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_JOS.34
	title = "eh_korea_JOS.34.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_JOS.34.d"
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
		
	trigger = {
		tag = KOR
		is_year = 1810
		NOT = { is_year = 1815 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_JOS.34.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		KOR = {
			set_country_flag = uprising_eh
			add_prestige = -10
			add_stability = -1
			add_corruption = 10
			add_adm_power = -50
			add_dip_power = -50
			add_mil_power = -50
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { area = pyongan_area }
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = pretender_rebels
					size = 1
					leader = "Hong Gyeong-nae"
				}
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { area = pyongan_area }
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = pretender_rebels
					size = 1
					leader = "Hong Gyeong-nae"
				}
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { area = pyongan_area }
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = pretender_rebels
					size = 1
					leader = "Hong Gyeong-nae"
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Peasant Revolts
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_JOS.35
	title = "eh_korea_JOS.35.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_JOS.35.d"
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = KOR
		is_year = 1850
		NOT = { is_year = 1860 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 700
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_JOS.35.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		KOR = {
			set_country_flag = uprising_eh
			add_stability = -1
			add_corruption = 10
			add_prestige = -10
			add_army_tradition = -10
			add_army_professionalism = -0.1
			add_faction_influence = {
				faction = nobles
				influence = 20
			}
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Byeon"
				dynasty = "Yi"
				change_adm = 1
				change_dip = 1
				change_mil = 1
				age = 19
				claim = 95
			}
			define_consort = {
				name = "Cheolin"
				dynasty = "Kim"
				change_adm = 2
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 2
				female = yes
			}
			remove_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
			every_owned_province = { add_unrest = 0.1 }
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { area = south_korea_area }
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = anti_tax_rebels
					size = 1
				}
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { area = south_korea_area }
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = anti_tax_rebels
					size = 1
				}
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { area = south_korea_area }
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = anti_tax_rebels
					size = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		tag = KOR

		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}

		days = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_JOS.36.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		KOR = {
			clr_country_flag = uprising_eh
			add_adm_power = 50
			add_dip_power = 50
			add_mil_power = 50
			add_stability = 1
			add_corruption = -10
			add_inflation = 1
			add_prestige = 10
			add_treasury = -10000
			disband_rebels = pretender_rebels
			disband_rebels = anti_tax_rebels
			735 = {
				add_great_project = {
					type = gyeongbok_palace
					instant = yes
				}
			}
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Ha-eung, Yi"
				change_adm = 4
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 3
				age = 40
				claim = 95
				regency = yes
			}
			define_heir = {
				name = "Hui"
				dynasty = "Yi"
				change_adm = 1
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 0
				age = 12
				claim = 95
			}
		}
	}
}

# French campaign
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_JOS.37
	title = "eh_korea_JOS.37.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_JOS.37.d"
	picture = ANZAC_COVE_LANDING_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = KOR
		is_year = 1865
		NOT = { is_year = 1867 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_JOS.37.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		FR2 = {
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = KOR
				casus_belli = cb_trade_conflict
			}
			country_event = { id = eh_french.51 days = 1 }
		}
		KOR = {
			add_sailors = -500
			country_event = { id = eh_korea_JOS.38 days = 100 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_JOS.37.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		KOR = {
			735 = { change_religion = catholic }
		}
	}
}

				discount = yes
			}

		}

			set_government_rank = 3

			add_mil_power = 100
			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = 10
			add_army_tradition = 10
			add_army_professionalism = 0.1
			korea_region = {
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = imperialism
					value = 10
				}
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = industrialization
					value = 10
				}
				add_institution_embracement = {
					which = nationalism_institution
					value = 40
				}
			}
		}
		QNG = {

			4653 = { change_culture = korean }
		}
	}
}

# Korean Armistice Agreement
country_event = {
	id = eh_korea_SKR.5
	title = "eh_korea_SKR.5.t"
	desc = "eh_korea_SKR.5.d"
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = SKO
		is_year = 1953
		NOT = { is_year = 1954 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			NOK = {
				pyongan_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = NOK }
					}
					cede_province = NOK
					add_core = NOK
					remove_core = SKO
				}
				hamgyeong_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = NOK }
					}
					cede_province = NOK
					add_core = NOK
					remove_core = SKO
				}
				western_korea_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = NOK }
							NOT = { province_id = 735 }
							NOT = { province_id = 4230 }
						}
					}
					cede_province = NOK
					add_core = NOK
					remove_core = SKO
				}
			}
			SKO = {
				south_korea_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = SKO }
					}
					cede_province = SKO
					add_core = SKO
					remove_core = NOK
				}
				eastern_korea_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { owned_by = SKO }
					}
					cede_province = SKO
					add_core = SKO
					remove_core = NOK
				}
				western_korea_area = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { owned_by = SKO }

						}
					}
					cede_province = SKO
					add_core = SKO
					remove_core = NOK
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_korea_SKR.5.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SKO = {
			clr_country_flag = korean_war
			add_prestige = -10
			set_capital = 735
			white_peace = NOK
			every_owned_province = { add_devastation = 80 }
		}
		NOK = {
			clr_country_flag = korean_war
			add_prestige = -10
			set_capital = 1845
			every_owned_province = { add_devastation = 80 }
			country_event = { id = eh_asia_KOR.16 days = 1 }
		}
		USA = {
			clr_country_flag = korean_war
			create_guarantee = SKO
			create_guarantee = FRM
			define_ruler = {
				name = "Dwight Eisenhower"
				change_adm = 3
				change_dip = 2
				change_mil = 5
				age = 63
			}
			country_event = { id = eh_USA.32 days = 1 }
		}
		GBR = {
			clr_country_flag = korean_war
			country_event = { id = eh_britain.70 days = 1 }
		}
		FR2 = {
			clr_country_flag = korean_war
			country_event = { id = eh_french.66 days = 1 }
		}
		CAN = {
			clr_country_flag = korean_war
			country_event = { id = eh_USA.32 days = 1 }
		}

			clr_country_flag = korean_war

            add_prestige = 50
			add_years_of_income = 5

				who = USA
				value = 50
				mutual = yes
			}

				who = USA
				modifier = sided_with_us
			}
		}

			add_stability = 1
			add_prestige = 50
			add_republican_tradition = 10
			add_opinion = {
				who = NOK
				modifier = sided_with_us
			}
		}
	}
}

# Spread of Buddhism to Korea 
country_event = {
	id = eh_asia_KOR.1
	title = "eh_asia_KOR.1.t"
	desc = "eh_asia_KOR.1.d"
	picture = BUDDHA_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			735 = { religion = mahayana }
			2745 = { religion = mahayana }
			1845 = { religion = mahayana }
			4201 = { religion = mahayana }
		}
		is_year = 370
		NOT = { is_year = 550 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1000
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_asia_KOR.1.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		GOG = {
			add_prestige = 10
			change_religion = mahayana
		}
		BKJ = {
			add_prestige = 10
			change_religion = mahayana
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_asia_KOR.1.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

# Spread of Confucianism to Korea 
country_event = {
	id = eh_asia_KOR.2
	title = "eh_asia_KOR.2.t"
	desc = "eh_asia_KOR.2.d"
	picture = RELIGIOUS_CONVERSION_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			culture_group = korean
			OR = {
				religion = mahayana
				religion = vajrayana
				NOT = { religion = confucianism }
			}
		}
		is_year = 950
		NOT = { is_year = 1880 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1000
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_asia_KOR.2.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		ROOT = {
			change_religion = confucianism
			add_harmonized_religion = mahayana
			add_prestige = 10
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_asia_KOR.2.b"
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		ROOT = { add_prestige = -10 }
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_asia_KOR.18.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

# Rise of the Goryeo - Event for tag
country_event = {
	id = eh_asia_KOR.19
	title = "eh_asia_KOR.19.t"
	desc = "eh_asia_KOR.19.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GOG
		is_year = 918
		NOT = { is_year = 920 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GOG = {
				clr_country_flag = eh_override_name
				restore_country_name = yes
				country_event = { id = eh_korea_HUSAMGUK.2 days = 3 }
			}
			GOR = {
				4231 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = GOR }
						}
					}
					rename_capital = "Songdo"
					cede_province = GOR
					add_core = GOR
					remove_core = GOG
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_asia_KOR.19.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				GOG = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = GOR
		}
	}
}

# Rise of the Joseon dynasty - Event for tag
country_event = {
	id = eh_asia_KOR.20
	title = "eh_asia_KOR.20.t"
	desc = "eh_asia_KOR.20.d"
	picture = IMPERIAL_SEAL_eventPicture
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GOR
		is_year = 1392
		NOT = { is_year = 1394 }
		has_global_flag = eh_historic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GOR = {
				every_owned_province = {
					change_culture = korean
					change_religion = confucianism
				}
				country_event = { id = eh_korea_JOS.1 days = 3 }
			}
			KOR = {
				735 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { owned_by = KOR }
						}
					}
					cede_province = KOR
					add_core = KOR
					remove_core = GOR
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "eh_asia_KOR.20.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				GOR = { was_player = yes }
			}
			switch_tag = KOR
		}
	}
}
